				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					21 Hungarian Dances (Piano), WoO 1 (Brahms, Johannes)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.25em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(245,245,245); width:80%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td width="42px" valign="top"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_notice.png" class="image"><img alt="Ambox notice.png" src="/images/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" width="40" height="40" /></a></td><td align="left">For the later orchestral versions of the dances, see <i><a href="/wiki/21_Hungarian_Dances_(Orchestra),_WoO_1_(Brahms,_Johannes)" title="21 Hungarian Dances (Orchestra), WoO 1 (Brahms, Johannes)">21 Hungarian Dances (Orchestra), WoO 1</a></i></td></tr></table></div>

<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>21 dances
</td></tr>

<th>Composition Year

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Version History
<ul><li> Composed for piano 4-hands, between 1858 and 1868 (Nos.1 to 10), 1879 (Nos.11 to 21)
</li><li> Nos.1 to 10 were arranged for solo piano by Brahms, 1872
</li><li> Nos.1, 3 and 10 were arranged for orchestra by Brahms, 1873 (first performance in this version: Lepizig, 5 February 1874; first published in 1874).
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
